                  <paragraph>
                     <content styleCode="Bold">Summary:</content>
                  </paragraph>
                  <paragraph>Your organization electronically submitted an initial case report to determine if reporting to public health is needed for a patient. "Zika virus disease (disorder)" is reportable to
                            "State Department of Health". An initial case report was sent to "State Department of Health". Additional information may be required for this report.<br />
                     <br />
                  </paragraph>
                  <paragraph>
                     <content styleCode="Bold">"Zika virus disease (disorder)" for "State Department of Health"</content>
                  </paragraph>
                  <paragraph>Reporting is required within "24 hours". Reporting to this Public Health Agency is based on "both patient home address and provider facility address". </paragraph>
                  <content>&gt; Local mosquito-borne Zika virus transmission was reported in your area. Increased watchfulness for symptoms of Zika virus in your patients is warranted. (Immediate action
                            requested)<br />
                     <br />
                  </content>
                  <content>&gt; Zika has particular risks for pregnant women. Follow-up guidance for pregnant women and couples who are planning pregnancy. (Immediate action requested)<br />
                     <br />
                  </content>
                  <content>&gt; Further Laboratory testing for Zika may be needed. Guidance for additional testing and specimen collection (Action requested)<br />
                     <br />
                  </content>
                  <content>&gt; Treatment guidance (Information only)<br />
                     <br />
                  </content>
                  <content>&gt; If you have additional questions regarding Zika or reporting, contact information for the State Department of Health is available here. (Information Only)<br />
                     <br />
